window.addEventListener('load',function(){
      var head=document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0],
      script=document.createElement('script');

      } else if (pageUrl.indexOf('pre') > -1) {
          srcUrl = 'https://psrpre.staticbg.com/rum/monitor.min.js';
      } else {
          srcUrl = 'https://psr.staticbg.com/rum/monitor.min.js';
      }
